---
about_this_resource_text: <p><strong>Description:&nbsp;</strong>Volumes and volume
  elements, covariant construction using the Levi-Civita tensor. How to go between
  differential and integral formulations of conservation laws. Electrodynamics in
  geometric language (4-current, Faraday field tensor). Introduction of the stress-energy
  tensor, with the perfect fluid stress-energy tensor as a particularly important
  example.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Prof. Scott Hughes</p>
course_id: 8-962-general-relativity-spring-2020

  <span m="216930">1.</span> <span m="218170">The fact</span> <span m="218350">that

  <span m="221040">us</span> <span m="221190">that</span> <span m="221310">it</span>
  <span m="221400">is</span> <span m="221520">timelike.</span></p><p><span m="231100">By</span>
  <span m="231250">the</span> <span m="231340">way,</span> <span m="231490">because</span>

  <span m="491020">particles.</span></p><p><span m="494810">So</span> <span m="494860">let's</span>
  <span m="495520">call</span> <span m="495820">this</span> <span m="496630">more</span>
  <span m="497050">interesting</span> <span m="497890">matter.</span> <span m="502800">So</span>
  <span m="503100">the</span> <span m="503250">simplest</span> <span m="505560">continuum</span>
  <span m="506160">form</span> <span m="506430">of</span> <span m="506520">matter</span>
  <span m="506790">which</span> <span m="506940">we're</span> <span m="507030">going</span>
  <span m="507170">to</span> <span m="507240">talk</span> <span m="507510">about</span>
  <span m="516330">is--</span> <span m="518030">we're</span> <span m="518220">going</span>
  <span m="518320">to</span> <span m="518429">call</span> <span m="518760">it</span>
  <span m="518909">dust.</span> <span m="519980">OK.</span> <span m="521679">When
  you're here</span> <span m="521820">at</span> <span m="521880">the</span> <span

  <span m="522900">get</span> <span m="522990">away</span> <span m="523200">with</span>
  <span m="523320">it,</span> <span m="523500">so you</span> <span m="523559">have</span>
  <span m="523650">an</span> <span m="523740">idea</span> <span m="523980">of</span>
  <span m="524070">what</span> <span m="524190">it</span> <span m="524250">means.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="534390">through</span> <span m="534480">each</span> <span m="534630">other.</span>

  <span m="799250">I</span> <span m="799310">described,</span> <span m="799790">when</span>

  <span m="2325060">the</span> <span m="2325180">Levi-Civita</span> <span m="2325770">symbol.</span></p><p><span
  m="2346110">So</span> <span m="2346390">that</span> <span m="2346570">3-volume</span>
  <span m="2347880">is</span> <span m="2348100">given</span> <span m="2348400">by</span>
  <span m="2351460">epsilon</span> <span m="2352000">ijk</span> <span m="2354060">Ai</span>
  <span m="2355220">Bj</span> <span m="2357100">Ck,</span> <span m="2358090">where--</span>
  <span m="2358780">I'll</span> <span m="2358870">remind</span> <span m="2359410">you--</span>
  <span m="2362210">epsilon</span> <span m="2362810">ijk</span> <span m="2364580">equals</span>
  <span m="2366200">plus</span> <span m="2366620">1</span> <span m="2367820">if</span>
  <span m="2368090">i</span> <span m="2368420">equals</span> <span m="2368840">1,</span>
  <span m="2369940">j</span> <span m="2370280">equals</span> <span m="2370700">2,</span>
  <span m="2372410">k</span> <span m="2372830">equals</span> <span m="2373200">3,</span>
  <span m="2376260">and</span> <span m="2376950">even</span> <span m="2377580">permutations.</span></p><p><span
  m="2383040">Even</span> <span m="2383280">permutations</span> <span m="2384000">means</span>
  <span m="2384240">I</span> <span m="2384300">swap</span> <span m="2384660">two</span>
  <span m="2384870">pairs</span> <span m="2385170">of</span> <span m="2385260">indices.</span>
  <span m="2385730">So</span> <span m="2386340">123,</span> <span m="2387600">231,</span>
  <span m="2389190">312--</span> <span m="2390090">those</span> <span m="2390300">all</span>
  <span m="2390420">give</span> <span m="2390600">me</span> <span m="2390720">plus</span>
  <span m="2391020">1.</span> <span m="2394320">It</span> <span m="2394410">gives</span>
  <span m="2394650">me</span> <span m="2394800">minus</span> <span m="2395430">1</span>
  <span m="2396090">for</span> <span m="2396300">any</span> <span m="2396720">odd</span>
  <span m="2396990">permutations</span> <span m="2397800">of</span> <span m="2397890">those.</span>
  <span m="2404230">So</span> <span m="2405430">132,</span> <span m="2407170">231,</span>
  <span m="2407620">et</span> <span m="2407860">cetera.</span> <span m="2408940">Those</span>
  <span m="2409120">will all</span> <span m="2409360">give</span> <span m="2409540">me</span>
  <span m="2409810">minus</span> <span m="2410320">1.</span> <span m="2411700">And</span>
  <span m="2412060">it's</span> <span m="2412270">0</span> <span m="2413170">if</span>
  <span m="2413320">any</span> <span m="2413530">index</span> <span m="2413830">is</span>
  <span m="2413960">repeated.</span></p><p><span m="2428630">So</span> <span m="2428780">you</span>

  <span m="4266840">to</span> <span m="4266930">0.</span> <span m="4267770">So</span>
  <span m="4267890">the</span> <span m="4267980">diagonal</span> <span m="4268460">becomes</span>
  <span m="4268880">zero,</span> <span m="4275070">and</span> <span m="4275250">only</span>
  <span m="4277900">the</span> <span m="4278310">six</span> <span m="4278760">off-diagonals</span>
  <span m="4279660">survive.</span></p><p><span m="4285210">And</span> <span m="4285400">then</span>
  <span m="4285490">you</span> <span m="4285550">go,</span> <span m="4286270">holy</span>
  <span m="4286480">crap.</span> <span m="4287050">Six.</span> <span m="4287740">That's</span>
  <span m="4287980">exactly</span> <span m="4288520">what</span> <span m="4288640">I</span>
  <span m="4288760">need</span> <span m="4289090">to</span> <span m="4289240">have</span>
  <span m="4289480">a</span> <span m="4289510">geometric</span> <span m="4289960">object</span>
  <span m="4290380">that</span> <span m="4290830">cleanly</span> <span m="4291400">holds</span>
  <span m="4292000">the</span> <span m="4292120">three</span> <span m="4292540">independent</span>
  <span m="4293080">electric</span> <span m="4293380">field</span> <span m="4293620">components</span>
  <span m="4294190">and</span> <span m="4294280">the</span> <span m="4294340">three</span>
  <span m="4294640">independent</span> <span m="4295420">magnetic</span> <span m="4295840">field</span>
  <span m="4296050">components.</span></p><p><span m="4297970">So</span> <span m="4299740">many</span>
  <span m="4299950">of</span> <span m="4300040">you</span> <span m="4300160">have</span>
  <span m="4300280">seen</span> <span m="4300580">all</span> <span m="4300700">this.</span>
